class=&quot;statement-end-if-in-editor&quot;></bdt> Such an offer wall allows third-party advertisers to offer virtual currency, gifts, or other items to users in return for the acceptance and completion of an advertisement offer. Such an offer wall may appear in our application(s) and be displayed to you based on certain data, such as your geographic area or demographic information. At this stage no uniform technology standard for <bdt class=&quot;block-component&quot;></bdt>recognizing<bdt class=&quot;statement-end-if-in-editor&quot;></bdt> and implementing DNT signals has been <bdt class=&quot;block-component&quot;></bdt>finalized<bdt class=&quot;statement-end-if-in-editor&quot;></bdt>. As such, we do not currently respond to DNT browser signals or any other mechanism that automatically communicates your choice not to be tracked online. If a standard for online tracking is adopted that we must follow in the future, we will inform you about that practice in a revised version of this privacy notice.</span></span></span></div><div style=&quot;line-height: 1.5;&quot;><br></div><div id=&quot;caresidents&quot; style=&quot;line-height: 1.5;&quot;><span style=&quot;color: rgb(127, 127, 127);&quot;><span style=&quot;color: rgb(89, 89, 89); font-size: 15px;&quot;><span style=&quot;font-size: 15px; color: rgb(89, 89, 89);&quot;><span style=&quot;font-size: 15px; color: rgb(89, 89, 89);&quot;><span id=&quot;control&quot; style=&quot;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);&quot;><strong><span data-custom-class=&quot;heading_1&quot;>10. DO CALIFORNIA RESIDENTS HAVE SPECIFIC PRIVACY RIGHTS?</span></strong></span></span></span></span></span></div><div style=&quot;line-height: 1.5;&quot;><br></div><div style=&quot;line-height: 1.5;&quot;><span style=&quot;font-size: 15px; color: rgb(89, 89, 89);&quot;><span style=&quot;font-size: 15px; color: rgb(89, 89, 89);&quot;><span data-custom-class=&quot;body_text&quot;><strong><em>In Short:&nbsp;</em></strong><em>Yes, if you are a resident of California, you are granted specific rights regarding access to your personal information.</em></span></span></span></div><div style=&quot;line-height: 1.5;&quot;><br></div><div style=&quot;line-height: 1.5;&quot;><span style=&quot;font-size: 15px; color: rgb(89, 89, 89);&quot;><span style=&quot;font-size: 15px; color: rgb(89, 89, 89);&quot;><span data-custom-class=&quot;body_text&quot;>California Civil Code Section 1798.83, also known as the <bdt class=&quot;block-component&quot;></bdt>&quot;Shine The Light&quot;<bdt class=&quot;statement-end-if-in-editor&quot;></bdt> law, permits our users who are California residents to request and obtain from us, once a year and free of charge, information about categories of personal information (if any) we disclosed to third parties for direct marketing purposes and the names and addresses of all third parties with which we shared personal information in the immediately preceding calendar year. If you are a California resident and would like to make such a request, please submit your request in writing to us using the contact information provided below.</span></span></span></div><div style=&quot;line-height: 1.5;&quot;><br></div><div style=&quot;line-height: 1.5;&quot;><span style=&quot;font-size: 15px; color: rgb(89, 89, 89);&quot;><span style=&quot;font-size: 15px; color: rgb(89, 89, 89);&quot;><span data-custom-class=&quot;body_text&quot;>If you are under 18 years of age, reside in California, and have a registered account with Services, you have the right to request removal of unwanted data that you publicly post on the Services. To request removal of such data, please contact us using the contact information provided below and include the email address associated with your account and a statement that you reside in California. We will make sure the data is not publicly displayed on the Services, but please be aware that the data may not be completely or comprehensively removed from all our systems (e.g.<bdt class=&quot;block-component&quot;></bdt>,<bdt class=&quot;statement-end-if-in-editor&quot;></bdt> backups, etc.).<span style=&quot;color: rgb(89, 89, 89); font-size: 15px;&quot;><span data-custom-class=&quot;body_text&quot;><bdt class=&quot;block-component&quot;></bdt></span></span></span></span></span></div><div style=&quot;line-height: 1.5;&quot;><br></div><div style=&quot;line-height: 1.5;&quot;><span data-custom-class=&quot;heading_2&quot; style=&quot;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);&quot;><span style=&quot;font-size: 15px;&quot;><strong>CCPA Privacy Notice</strong></span></span></div><div><div><br></div><div style=&quot;line-height: 1.5;&quot;><span style=&quot;color: rgb(127, 127, 127);&quot;><span style=&quot;color: rgb(89, 89, 89); margin-left: 20px;&quot;><span style=&quot;font-size: 15px; color: rgb(89, 89, 89);&quot;><span style=&quot;font-size: 15px; color: rgb(89, 89, 89);&quot;><span data-custom-class=&quot;body_text&quot;>(2) every individual who is domiciled in the State of California who is outside the State of California for a temporary or transitory purpose</span></span></span></div><div style=&quot;line-height: 1.5;&quot;><br></div><div style=&quot;line-height: 1.5;&quot;><span style=&quot;font-size: 15px; color: rgb(89, 89, 89);&quot;><span style=&quot;font-size: 15px; color: rgb(89, 89, 89);&quot;><span data-custom-class=&quot;body_text&quot;>All other individuals are defined as <bdt class=&quot;block-component&quot;></bdt>&quot;non-residents.&quot;<bdt class=&quot;statement-end-if-in-editor&quot;></bdt></span></span></span></div><div style=&quot;line-height: 1.5;&quot;><br></div><div style=&quot;line-height: 1.5;&quot;><span style=&quot;font-size: 15px; color: rgb(89, 89, 89);&quot;><span style=&quot;font-size: 15px; color: rgb(89, 89, 89);&quot;><span data-custom-class=&quot;body_text&quot;>Upon receiving your request, we will need to verify your identity to determine you are the same person about whom we have the information in our system. These verification efforts require us to ask you to provide information so that we can match it with information you have previously provided us. For instance, depending on the type of request you submit, we may ask you to provide certain information so that we can match the information you provide with the information we already have on file, or we may contact you through a communication method (e.g.<bdt class=&quot;block-component&quot;></bdt>,<bdt class=&quot;statement-end-if-in-editor&quot;></bdt> phone or email) that you have previously provided to us. It does not include a natural person acting in a commercial or employment context.</span></span></div><div style=&quot;line-height: 1.5;&quot;><span style=&quot;font-size: 15px;&quot;><br></span></div><div style=&quot;line-height: 1.5;&quot;><span style=&quot;font-size: 15px;&quot;><span data-custom-class=&quot;body_text&quot;><bdt class=&quot;block-component&quot;></bdt>&quot;Personal data&quot;<bdt class=&quot;statement-end-if-in-editor&quot;></bdt> means any information that is linked or reasonably linkable to an identified or identifiable natural person. <bdt class=&quot;block-component&quot;></bdt>&quot;Personal data&quot;<bdt class=&quot;statement-end-if-in-editor&quot;></bdt> does not include de-identified data or publicly available information.</span></span></div><div style=&quot;line-height: 1.5;&quot;><span style=&quot;font-size: 15px;&quot;><br></span></div><div style=&quot;line-height: 1.5;&quot;><span class=&quot;statement-end-if-in-editor&quot;></bdt> means the exchange of personal data for monetary consideration.</span></span></div><div style=&quot;line-height: 1.5;&quot;><span
